### [463] [CEMR: An Effective Subgraph Matching Algorithm with Redundant Extension Elimination](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08037)
*Linglin Yang,Xunbin Su,Lei Zou,Xiangyang Gou,Yinnian Lin*

Main category: cs.DB

TL;DR: CEMR是一种新的子图匹配算法，通过合并和重用公共扩展来减少重复计算，并采用剪枝技术提高效率，在真实世界数据集上优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 子图匹配是图分析中的基本问题，但由于其NP难特性，在大规模真实世界图上高效枚举子图匹配仍然极具挑战。现有深度优先搜索回溯策略存在大量重复计算，增加了整体运行时间。

Method: 提出CEMR算法，包含两种减少重复扩展的技术：1) 利用黑白顶点编码的公共扩展合并；2) 使用公共扩展缓冲区的公共扩展重用。此外，设计了两种剪枝技术来丢弃无希望的搜索分支。

Result: 在真实世界数据集和多样化查询工作负载上的广泛实验表明，CEMR优于最先进的子图匹配方法。

Conclusion: CEMR通过有效减少重复计算和剪枝无希望分支，显著提高了子图匹配的效率，为大规模图分析提供了更高效的解决方案。

Abstract: Subgraph matching is a fundamental problem in graph analysis with a wide range of applications. However, due to its inherent NP-hardness, enumerating subgraph matches efficiently on large real-world graphs remains highly challenging. Most existing works adopt a depth-first search (DFS) backtracking strategy, where a partial embedding is gradually extended in a DFS manner along a branch of the search trees until either a full embedding is found or no further extension is possible. A major limitation of this paradigm is the significant amount of duplicate computation that occurs during enumeration, which increases the overall runtime. To overcome this limitation, we propose a novel subgraph matching algorithm, CEMR. It incorporates two techniques to reduce duplicate extensions: common extension merging, which leverages a black-white vertex encoding, and common extension reusing, which employs common extension buffers. In addition, we design two pruning techniques to discard unpromising search branches. Extensive experiments on real-world datasets and diverse query workloads demonstrate that CEMR outperforms state-of-the-art subgraph matching methods.

</details>


### [464] [PRIME: Efficient Algorithm for Token Graph Routing Problem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08337)
*Haotian Xu,Yuqing Zhu,Yuming Huang,Jing Tang*

Main category: cs.DB

TL;DR: PRIME是一个两阶段迭代图算法，用于解决区块链资产交换中的Token Graph Routing Problem (TGRP)，通过剪枝图搜索和凸优化显著提升交易执行价格和计算效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 区块链驱动的资产交换平台提出了新颖的图查询优化问题，现有解决方案由于边缘权重由凹交换函数定义的非线性特性而效率低下，需要更有效的路由算法。

Method: 提出PRIME两阶段算法：第一阶段使用剪枝图搜索高效识别高潜力路由路径；第二阶段将分配任务建模为强凸优化问题，使用新颖的自适应符号梯度方法(ASGM)以线性收敛率求解。

Result: 在真实以太坊数据上的实验显示，PRIME相比行业基准Uniswap路由算法，在大额交易中实现高达8.42个基点的更好执行价格，同时减少高达96.7%的计算量，已在对冲基金生产环境中部署验证。

Conclusion: PRIME为高频去中心化市场提供了一个可扩展的图查询处理解决方案，通过创新的两阶段算法有效解决了Token Graph Routing Problem，在实际应用中表现出优越的性能和实用性。

Abstract: Optimizing asset exchanges on blockchain-driven platforms poses a novel and challenging graph query optimization problem. In this model, assets represent vertices and exchanges form edges, recasting the graph query task as a routing problem over a large-scale, dynamic graph. However, the existing solutions fail to solve the problem efficiently due to the non-linear nature of the edge weights defined by a concave swap function. To address the challenge, we propose PRIME, a two-stage iterative graph algorithm designed for the Token Graph Routing Problem (TGRP). The first stage employs a pruned graph search to efficiently identify a set of high-potential routing paths. The second stage formulates the allocation task as a strongly convex optimization problem, which we solve using our novel Adaptive Sign Gradient Method (ASGM) with a linear convergence rate. Extensive experiments on real-world Ethereum data confirm PRIME's advantages over industry baselines. PRIME consistently outperforms the widely-used Uniswap routing algorithm, achieving up to 8.42 basis points (bps) better execution prices on large trades while reducing computation up to 96.7%. The practicality of PRIME is further validated by its deployment in hedge fund production environments, demonstrating its viability as a scalable graph query processing solution for high-frequency decentralized markets.

</details>


### [465] [LLM-Driven Online Aggregation for Unstructured Text Analytics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08443)
*Chao Hui,Weizheng Lu,Yanjie Gao,Lingfeng Xiong,Yunhai Wang,Yueguo Chen*

Main category: cs.DB

TL;DR: OLLA：基于LLM的在线聚合框架，通过语义分层采样和渐进式处理加速语义数据处理，相比全数据处理实现1.6-38倍加速。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM在文本处理方面表现出色，但基于LLM的数据处理受限于token生成速度较慢，无法满足实时响应需求。现有批处理系统需要处理完整数据集后才能输出结果，缺乏渐进式处理能力。

Method: 提出OLLA框架：1）将文本增量转换为结构化数据流；2）应用在线聚合提供渐进式输出；3）引入语义分层采样方法优化数据选择，加速收敛到真实值。

Result: 评估显示：OLLA仅用不到4%的全数据处理时间就能达到1%的准确度误差边界；在达到5%误差边界的时间上，相比全数据处理实现了1.6倍到38倍的加速。

Conclusion: OLLA通过在线聚合和语义分层采样有效解决了LLM数据处理的速度瓶颈，显著提升了实时响应能力，为LLM驱动的数据分析提供了高效解决方案。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) exhibit strong capabilities in text processing, and recent research has augmented SQL and DataFrame with LLM-powered semantic operators for data analysis. However, LLM-based data processing is hindered by slower token generation speeds compared to relational queries. To enhance real-time responsiveness, we propose OLLA, an LLM-driven online aggregation framework that accelerates semantic processing within relational queries. In contrast to batch-processing systems that yield results only after the entire dataset is processed, our approach incrementally transforms text into a structured data stream and applies online aggregation to provide progressive output. To enhance our online aggregation process, we introduce a semantic stratified sampling approach that improves data selection and expedites convergence to the ground truth. Evaluations show that OLLA reaches 1% accuracy error bound compared with labeled ground truth using less than 4% of the full-data time. It achieves speedups ranging from 1.6$\times$ to 38$\times$ across diverse domains, measured by comparing the time to reach a 5% error bound with that of full-data time. We release our code at https://github.com/olla-project/llm-online-agg.git.

</details>


### [466] [Query-Guided Analysis and Mitigation of Data Verification Errors (Extended Version)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08612)
*Ran Schreiber,Yael Amsterdamer*

Main category: cs.DB

TL;DR: 提出一个评估数据验证错误对查询结果影响的框架，引入最大错误分数(MES)和最坏情况不确定性度量，开发算法检测风险元组并指导额外验证步骤


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 数据验证是数据驱动流程中的关键预处理步骤，但现有验证工具仍可能产生错误标签，这些错误会以复杂方式传播到下游查询结果中，影响结果可靠性

Method: 提出一个框架，引入最大错误分数(MES)作为最坏情况不确定性度量，识别风险元组，开发MESReduce算法与外部验证器交互，选择有效的额外验证步骤

Result: 在真实和合成数据集上的评估表明，MESReduce能显著有效地降低MES，提高验证结果的准确性

Conclusion: 该框架能补充现有验证工具，通过评估标签错误对查询输出的影响，指导额外验证步骤，从而提高结果可靠性

Abstract: Data verification, the process of labeling data items as correct or incorrect, is a preprocessing step that may critically affect the quality of results in data-driven pipelines. Despite recent advances, verification can still produce erroneous labels that propagate to downstream query results in complex ways. We present a framework that complements existing verification tools by assessing the impact of potential labeling errors on query outputs and guiding additional verification steps to improve result reliability. To this end, we introduce Maximal Error Score (MES), a worst-case uncertainty metric that quantifies the reliability of query output tuples independently of the underlying data distribution. As an auxiliary indicator, we identify risky tuples - input tuples for which reducing label uncertainty may counterintuitively increase the output uncertainty. We then develop efficient algorithms for computing MES and detecting risky tuples, as well as a generic algorithm, named MESReduce, that builds on both indicators and interacts with external verifiers to select effective additional verification steps. We implement our techniques in a prototype system and evaluate them on real and synthetic datasets, demonstrating that MESReduce can substantially and effectively reduce the MES and improve the accuracy of verification results.

</details>
